I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[FEATURE] MCP redirects
**Is your feature request related to a problem? Please describe.**
When trying to connect to an MCP server that has been moved and is issuing a temp redirect status, the client is coded to refuse to follow the redirect. This causes the connection to fail - with no available mitigation strategy. 

**Describe the solution you'd like**
One of:
The ability to specify that the http client follows redirects in the builder.
Redirects on by default (yeah yeah breaking change)
The ability to provide my own httpclient in the builder.

**Describe alternatives you've considered**
Inherit from the StreamableHttpMcpTransport class and roll my own. I'd rather not but this is quite the roadblock for me.

**Additional context**
The issue is in dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.transport.http.StreamableHttpMcpTransport at line 163. 
The sendAsync is getting a 307 in the response status code at line 165 and it ends up down at 222 with java.lang.RuntimeException: Unexpected status code: 307. 

In my case the mcp server is working perfectly but it's been moved. 
It's not mine so I can't do anything about that. 
There's no way to set the httpClient to allow redirects and the default is NEVER.

</pr_description>

    66	    public StreamableHttpMcpTransport(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder builder) {
    67	        url = ensureNotNull(builder.url, "Missing server endpoint URL");
    68	        logRequests = builder.logRequests;
    69	        logResponses = builder.logResponses;
    70	        trafficLog = getOrDefault(builder.logger, McpLoggers.traffic());
    71	        Duration timeout = getOrDefault(builder.timeout, Duration.ofSeconds(60));
    72	        customHeadersSupplier = getOrDefault(builder.customHeadersSupplier, (i) -> Map.of());
    73	        sslContext = builder.sslContext;
    74	        httpVersion = builder.forceHttpVersion1_1 ? HttpClient.Version.HTTP_1_1 : HttpClient.Version.HTTP_2;
    75	        subsidiaryChannelEnabled = builder.subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
    76	        executor = getOrDefault(builder.executor, DefaultExecutorProvider.getDefaultExecutorService());
    77	        HttpClient.Builder clientBuilder =
    78	                HttpClient.newBuilder().connectTimeout(timeout).version(httpVersion);
    79	        if (builder.executor != null) {
    80	            clientBuilder.executor(builder.executor);
    81	        }
    82	        if (sslContext != null) {
    83	            clientBuilder.sslContext(sslContext);
    84	        }
    85	        httpClient = clientBuilder.build();
    86	    }

    93	    @Override
    94	    public CompletableFuture<JsonNode> initialize(McpInitializeRequest operation) {
    95	        this.initializeRequest = operation;
    96	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> completableFuture = execute(new McpCallContext(null, operation), false);
    97	        initializeInProgress.set(completableFuture);
    98	        return completableFuture
    99	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   100	                    initializeInProgress.set(null);
   101	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   102	                })
   103	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> execute(
   104	                                new McpCallContext(null, new McpInitializationNotification()), false)
   105	                        .thenCompose(nullNode -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse)))
   106	                .thenCompose(originalResponse -> {
   107	                    if (subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   108	                        return startSubsidiaryChannel(true)
   109	                                .thenCompose(v -> CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse));
   110	                    }
   111	                    return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(originalResponse);
   112	                });
   113	    }

   115	    private HttpRequest createRequest(McpJsonRpcMessage message, McpCallContext callContext)
   116	            throws JsonProcessingException {
   117	        String body = OBJECT_MAPPER.writeValueAsString(message);
   118	        HttpRequest.BodyPublisher bodyPublisher = HttpRequest.BodyPublishers.ofString(body);
   119	        if (logRequests) {
   120	            trafficLog.info("Request: {}", body);
   121	        }
   122	        final HttpRequest.Builder builder = HttpRequest.newBuilder();
   123	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   124	        if (sessionId != null && !(message instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   125	            builder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   126	        }
   127	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(callContext);
   128	        if (headers != null) {
   129	            headers.forEach(builder::header);
   130	        }
   131	        return builder.uri(URI.create(url))
   132	                .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
   133	                .header("Accept", "application/json,text/event-stream")
   134	                .POST(bodyPublisher)
   135	                .build();
   136	    }

   168	    private CompletableFuture<JsonNode> execute(McpCallContext context, boolean isRetry) {
   169	        Long id = context.message().getId();
   170	        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest)) {
   171	            CompletableFuture<JsonNode> reinitializeInProgress = this.initializeInProgress.get();
   172	            if (reinitializeInProgress != null) {
   173	                reinitializeInProgress.join();
   174	            }
   175	        }
   176	        HttpRequest request = null;
   177	        try {
   178	            request = createRequest(
   179	                    context.message(), new McpCallContext(context.invocationContext(), context.message()));
   180	        } catch (JsonProcessingException e) {
   181	            return CompletableFuture.failedFuture(e);
   182	        }
   183	        CompletableFuture<JsonNode> future = new CompletableFuture<>();
   184	        if (id != null) {
   185	            operationHandler.startOperation(id, future);
   186	        }
   187	
   188	        httpClient
   189	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   190	                    if (!isExpectedStatusCode(responseInfo.statusCode())) {
   191	                        if (!(context.message() instanceof McpInitializeRequest) && responseInfo.statusCode() == 404) {
   192	                            if (!isRetry) {
   193	                                initialize(StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.initializeRequest)
   194	                                        .thenAccept(node -> {
   195	                                            execute(context, true)
   196	                                                    .thenAccept(future::complete)
   197	                                                    .exceptionally(t -> {
   198	                                                        future.completeExceptionally(t);
   199	                                                        return null;
   200	                                                    });
   201	                                        })
   202	                                        .exceptionally(t -> {
   203	                                            future.completeExceptionally(t);
   204	                                            return null;
   205	                                        });
   206	                            }
   207	                        } else {
   208	                            future.completeExceptionally(
   209	                                    new RuntimeException("Unexpected status code: " + responseInfo.statusCode()));
   210	                        }
   211	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   212	                    } else {
   213	                        Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   214	                        Optional<String> mcpSessionId = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Mcp-Session-Id");
   215	                        if (mcpSessionId.isPresent()) {
   216	                            LOG.debug("Assigned MCP session ID: {}", mcpSessionId);
   217	                            StreamableHttpMcpTransport.this.mcpSessionId.set(mcpSessionId.get());
   218	                        }
   219	                        if (id != null
   220	                                && contentType.isPresent()
   221	                                && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   222	                            // the server has started an SSE stream
   223	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(
   224	                                    new SseSubscriber(future, logResponses, operationHandler, trafficLog));
   225	                        } else {
   226	                            // the server has returned a regular HTTP response
   227	                            return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.mapping(
   228	                                    HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.ofString(StandardCharsets.UTF_8), responseBody -> {
   229	                                        if (logResponses) {
   230	                                            trafficLog.info("Response: {}", responseBody);
   231	                                        }
   232	                                        if (id == null) {
   233	                                            future.complete(null);
   234	                                        }
   235	                                        try {
   236	                                            JsonNode node = OBJECT_MAPPER.readTree(responseBody);
   237	                                            operationHandler.handle(node);
   238	                                            return null;
   239	                                        } catch (IOException e) {
   240	                                            future.completeExceptionally(e);
   241	                                            return null;
   242	                                        }
   243	                                    });
   244	                        }
   245	                    }
   246	                })
   247	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   248	                    future.completeExceptionally(t);
   249	                    return null;
   250	                });
   251	        return future;
   252	    }
   253	
   254	    /**
   255	     * Opens the subsidiary SSE channel by issuing an HTTP GET to the MCP endpoint.
   256	     * This allows the server to send notifications and requests to the client
   257	     * without the client first sending data via HTTP POST.
   258	     *
   259	     * @param firstAttempt if true, failures will not trigger reconnection
   260	     * @return a future that completes when the channel setup attempt finishes
   261	     */
   262	    private CompletableFuture<Void> startSubsidiaryChannel(boolean firstAttempt) {
   263	        if (closed.get()) {
   264	            return CompletableFuture.completedFuture(null);
   265	        }
   266	        HttpRequest.Builder requestBuilder = HttpRequest.newBuilder()
   267	                .uri(URI.create(url))
   268	                .header("Accept", "text/event-stream")
   269	                .GET();
   270	        String sessionId = mcpSessionId.get();
   271	        if (sessionId != null) {
   272	            requestBuilder.header("Mcp-Session-Id", sessionId);
   273	        }
   274	        String lastId = subsidiaryLastEventId.get();
   275	        if (lastId != null) {
   276	            requestBuilder.header("Last-Event-ID", lastId);
   277	        }
   278	        Map<String, String> headers = customHeadersSupplier.apply(null);
   279	        if (headers != null) {
   280	            headers.forEach(requestBuilder::header);
   281	        }
   282	        HttpRequest request = requestBuilder.build();
   283	
   284	        CompletableFuture<Void> result = new CompletableFuture<>();
   285	        SseSubscriber subscriber = new SseSubscriber(
   286	                logResponses,
   287	                operationHandler,
   288	                trafficLog,
   289	                subsidiaryLastEventId,
   290	                subsidiaryRetryMs,
   291	                this::scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect,
   292	                closed);
   293	
   294	        httpClient
   295	                .sendAsync(request, responseInfo -> {
   296	                    int statusCode = responseInfo.statusCode();
   297	                    Optional<String> contentType = responseInfo.headers().firstValue("Content-Type");
   298	                    if (isExpectedStatusCode(statusCode)
   299	                            && contentType.isPresent()
   300	                            && contentType.get().contains("text/event-stream")) {
   301	                        subsidiaryChannelEstablished = true;
   302	                        LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel established");
   303	                        result.complete(null);
   304	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.fromLineSubscriber(subscriber);
   305	                    } else {
   306	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   307	                            LOG.warn(
   308	                                    "Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), will not re-attempt",
   309	                                    statusCode,
   310	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   311	                        } else {
   312	                            LOG.debug(
   313	                                    "Failed to reconnect subsidiary SSE channel (status={}, contentType={}), scheduling retry",
   314	                                    statusCode,
   315	                                    contentType.orElse("absent"));
   316	                            if (!closed.get()) {
   317	                                scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   318	                            }
   319	                        }
   320	                        result.complete(null);
   321	                        return HttpResponse.BodySubscribers.discarding();
   322	                    }
   323	                })
   324	                .exceptionally(t -> {
   325	                    if (!closed.get()) {
   326	                        if (firstAttempt) {
   327	                            LOG.warn("Failed to open subsidiary SSE channel", t);
   328	                        } else {
   329	                            LOG.debug("Subsidiary SSE channel connection failed, scheduling retry", t);
   330	                            scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect();
   331	                        }
   332	                    }
   333	                    result.complete(null);
   334	                    return null;
   335	                });
   336	        return result;
   337	    }
   338	
   339	    private void scheduleSubsidiaryReconnect() {
   340	        if (closed.get() || !subsidiaryChannelEstablished) {

   355	    private boolean isExpectedStatusCode(int statusCode) {
   356	        return statusCode >= 200 && statusCode < 300;

   359	    @Override
   360	    public void close() throws IOException {
   361	        closed.set(true);
   362	        // The httpClient.close() method only exists on JDK 21+, so invoke it only if we can.
   363	        // Replace this with a normal method call when switching the base to JDK 21+.
   364	        try {
   365	            httpClient.getClass().getMethod("close").invoke(httpClient);
   366	        } catch (NoSuchMethodException | IllegalAccessException | InvocationTargetException ignored) {
   367	        }
   368	    }

   402	
   403	        /**
   404	         * A supplier for dynamic request headers of the MCP server.
   405	         * The supplier is called for each request, allowing headers to be updated dynamically.
   406	         */
   407	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder customHeaders(Supplier<Map<String, String>> customHeadersSupplier) {
   408	            this.customHeadersSupplier = i -> customHeadersSupplier.get();
   409	            return this;
   410	        }
   411	
   412	        /**
   413	         * A supplier for dynamic request headers of the MCP server.
   414	         * The supplier is called for each request, allowing headers to be updated dynamically.
   415	         */
   416	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder customHeaders(McpHeadersSupplier customHeadersSupplier) {
   417	            this.customHeadersSupplier = customHeadersSupplier;
   418	            return this;
   419	        }
   420	
   421	        /**
   422	         * The connection timeout (applied on the http client level). Application-level
   423	         * timeouts are handled by the MCP client itself.
   424	         */
   425	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder timeout(Duration timeout) {
   426	            this.timeout = timeout;
   427	            return this;
   428	        }
   429	
   430	        /**
   431	         * Whether to log all requests that are sent over this transport.
   432	         */
   433	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder logRequests(boolean logRequests) {
   434	            this.logRequests = logRequests;
   435	            return this;
   436	        }
   437	
   438	        /**
   439	         * Whether to log all responses received over this transport.
   440	         */
   441	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder logResponses(boolean logResponses) {
   442	            this.logResponses = logResponses;
   443	            return this;
   444	        }
   445	
   446	        /**
   447	         * Sets a custom {@link Logger} to be used for traffic logging (both requests and responses).
   448	         * This logger will be used for both regular HTTP responses and Server-Sent Events (SSE) traffic.
   449	         * If not specified, a default logger will be used.
   450	         *
   451	         * @param logger an alternate {@link Logger} to be used instead of the default one provided by Langchain4J for traffic logging.
   452	         * @return {@code this}.
   453	         */
   454	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder logger(Logger logger) {
   455	            this.logger = logger;
   456	            return this;
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        /**
   460	         * An optional {@link Executor} that will be used for executing requests and handling responses.
   461	         * It will also be used for scheduling auto-reconnect attempts of the subsidiary SSE channel if that is enabled.
   462	         * If not provided, a default shared executor will be used.
   463	         */
   464	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder executor(Executor executor) {
   465	            this.executor = executor;
   466	            return this;
   467	        }
   468	
   469	        /**
   470	         * Supplies a custom {@link SSLContext} used when establishing HTTPS connections to the MCP server,
   471	         * allowing private CAs or certificates.
   472	         */
   473	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder sslContext(SSLContext sslContext) {
   474	            this.sslContext = sslContext;
   475	            return this;
   476	        }
   477	
   478	        /**
   479	         * Forces the transport to use HTTP/1.1 instead of the default HTTP/2.
   480	         */
   481	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder setHttpVersion1_1() {
   482	            this.forceHttpVersion1_1 = true;
   483	            return this;
   484	        }
   485	
   486	        /**
   487	         * Enables or disables the subsidiary SSE channel. When enabled, the transport
   488	         * will open an HTTP GET-based SSE stream after initialization, allowing the
   489	         * server to send notifications and requests to the client without the client
   490	         * first sending data via HTTP POST. If the server does not support the
   491	         * subsidiary channel (returns 405), the transport will log a warning and
   492	         * continue without it. If the stream breaks after being successfully
   493	         * established, the transport will automatically attempt to reconnect.
   494	         * Defaults to {@code false}.
   495	         */
   496	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder subsidiaryChannel(boolean subsidiaryChannelEnabled) {
   497	            this.subsidiaryChannelEnabled = subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
   498	            return this;
   499	        }
   500	
   501	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport build() {
   502	            return new StreamableHttpMcpTransport(this);
   503	        }
   504	    }
   505	}

     9	    @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
    10	    public final McpClientMethod method;
    11	
    12	    public McpClientMessage(Long id, McpClientMethod method) {
    13	        super(id);
    14	        this.method = method;
    15	    }
    16	}
     1	package dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.transport;
     2	
     3	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
     4	import dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.McpRoot;
     5	import dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.logging.McpLogMessage;
     6	import dev.langchain4j.mcp.protocol.McpPingResponse;
     7	import dev.langchain4j.mcp.protocol.McpRootsListResponse;
     8	import java.util.List;
     9	import java.util.Map;
    10	import java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture;
    11	import java.util.function.Consumer;
    12	import java.util.function.Supplier;
    13	import org.slf4j.Logger;
    14	import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * Handles incoming messages from the MCP server. Transport implementations
    18	 * should call the "handle" method on each received message. A transport also has
    19	 * to call "startOperation" when before starting an operation that requires a response
    20	 * to register its ID in the map of pending operations.
    21	 */
    22	public class McpOperationHandler {
    23	
    24	    private final Map<Long, CompletableFuture<JsonNode>> pendingOperations;
    25	    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(McpOperationHandler.class);
    26	    private final McpTransport transport;
    27	    private final Consumer<McpLogMessage> logMessageConsumer;
    28	    private final Runnable onToolListUpdate;
    29	    private final Supplier<List<McpRoot>> roots;
    30	
    31	    public McpOperationHandler(
    32	            Map<Long, CompletableFuture<JsonNode>> pendingOperations,
    33	            Supplier<List<McpRoot>> roots,
    34	            McpTransport transport,
    35	            Consumer<McpLogMessage> logMessageConsumer,
    36	            Runnable onToolListUpdate) {
    37	        this.pendingOperations = pendingOperations;
    38	        this.transport = transport;
    39	        this.logMessageConsumer = logMessageConsumer;
    40	        this.onToolListUpdate = onToolListUpdate;
    41	        this.roots = roots;
    42	    }
    43	
    44	    public void handle(JsonNode message) {
    45	        if (message.has("id")) {
    46	            long messageId = message.get("id").asLong();
    47	            if (message.has("result") || message.has("error")) {
    48	                // if there is a result or error, we assume that this is related to a client-initiated operation
    49	                CompletableFuture<JsonNode> op = pendingOperations.remove(messageId);
    50	                if (op != null) {
    51	                    op.complete(message);
    52	                } else {
    53	                    log.warn("Received response for unknown message id: {}", messageId);
    54	                }
    55	            } else {
    56	                // this is a server-initiated operation, the pendingOperations map is not relevant
    57	                if (message.has("method")) {
    58	                    String method = message.get("method").asText();
    59	                    if (method.equals("ping")) {
    60	                        transport.executeOperationWithoutResponse(new McpPingResponse(messageId));
    61	                        return;
    62	                    } else if (method.equals("roots/list")) {
    63	                        transport.executeOperationWithoutResponse(new McpRootsListResponse(messageId, roots.get()));
    64	                        return;
    65	                    }
    66	                }
    67	                log.warn("Received response for unknown message id: {}", messageId);
    68	            }
    69	        } else if (message.has("method")) {
    70	            String method = message.get("method").asText();
    71	            if (method.equals("notifications/message")) {
    72	                // this is a log message
    73	                if (message.has("params")) {
    74	                    if (logMessageConsumer != null) {
    75	                        logMessageConsumer.accept(McpLogMessage.fromJson(message.get("params")));
    76	                    }
    77	                } else {
    78	                    log.warn("Received log message without params: {}", message);
    79	                }
    80	            } else if (method.equals("notifications/tools/list_changed")) {
    81	                onToolListUpdate.run();
    82	            } else {
    83	                log.warn("Received unknown message: {}", message);
    84	            }
    85	        }
    86	    }
    87	
    88	    public void startOperation(Long id, CompletableFuture<JsonNode> future) {
    89	        pendingOperations.put(id, future);
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    public synchronized void cancelAllPendingOperations(String reason) {
    93	        for (CompletableFuture<JsonNode> future : pendingOperations.values()) {
    94	            future.completeExceptionally(
    95	                    new IllegalStateException("Operation cancelled due to transport failure: " + reason));
    96	        }
    97	        pendingOperations.clear();
    98	    }
    99	}

     3	import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;
     4	
     5	import dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.transport.http.StreamableHttpMcpTransport;

     9	import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
    10	
    11	class StreamableHttpMcpTransportTest {
    12	
    13	    @Test
    14	    void shouldApplyCustomSslContext() throws Exception {
    15	        SSLContext customContext = SSLContext.getInstance("TLS");
    16	        customContext.init(null, null, null);
    17	
    18	        StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.builder()
    19	                .url("http://localhost/mcp")
    20	                .sslContext(customContext)
    21	                .build();
    22	
    23	        assertThat(extractSslContext(transport)).isSameAs(customContext);
    24	    }
    25	
    26	    @Test
    27	    void shouldUseHttp2ByDefault() throws Exception {
    28	        StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport =
    29	                StreamableHttpMcpTransport.builder().url("http://localhost/mcp").build();
    30	
    31	        assertThat(extractHttpClient(transport).version()).isEqualTo(HttpClient.Version.HTTP_2);
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    @Test
    35	    void shouldForceHttp11ForStreamableTransport() throws Exception {
    36	        StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.builder()
    37	                .url("http://localhost/mcp")
    38	                .setHttpVersion1_1()
    39	                .build();
    40	
    41	        assertThat(extractHttpClient(transport).version()).isEqualTo(HttpClient.Version.HTTP_1_1);
    42	    }
    43	
    44	    private static SSLContext extractSslContext(StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport) throws Exception {
    45	        Field field = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.class.getDeclaredField("sslContext");
    46	        field.setAccessible(true);
    47	        return (SSLContext) field.get(transport);
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    private static HttpClient extractHttpClient(StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport) throws Exception {
    51	        Field field = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.class.getDeclaredField("httpClient");
    52	        field.setAccessible(true);
    53	        return (HttpClient) field.get(transport);
    54	    }
    55	}

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.sun.net.httpserver.HttpServer;
import dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.transport.McpOperationHandler;
import dev.langchain4j.mcp.client.transport.http.StreamableHttpMcpTransport;
import dev.langchain4j.mcp.protocol.McpInitializeRequest;
import java.io.OutputStream;
import java.net.InetSocketAddress;
import java.net.URI;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.concurrent.*;

public class ReproMcpRedirect {
  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    HttpServer server = HttpServer.create(new InetSocketAddress("127.0.0.1", 0), 0);
    server.createContext("/old", exchange -> {
      URI newUri = URI.create("http://127.0.0.1:" + server.getAddress().getPort() + "/new");
      exchange.getResponseHeaders().add("Location", newUri.toString());
      exchange.sendResponseHeaders(307, -1);
      exchange.close();
    });
    server.createContext("/new", exchange -> {
      byte[] body = "{\"jsonrpc\":\"2.0\",\"id\":1,\"result\":{}}".getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
      exchange.getResponseHeaders().add("Content-Type", "application/json");
      exchange.sendResponseHeaders(200, body.length);
      try (OutputStream os = exchange.getResponseBody()) { os.write(body); }
    });
    server.start();
    try {
      String url = "http://127.0.0.1:" + server.getAddress().getPort() + "/old";
      StreamableHttpMcpTransport transport = StreamableHttpMcpTransport.builder().url(url).build();
      transport.start(new McpOperationHandler(new ConcurrentHashMap<>(), List::of, transport, null, () -> {}));
      CompletableFuture<JsonNode> response = transport.executeOperationWithResponse(new McpInitializeRequest(1L));
      try {
        System.out.println(response.get(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS));
      } catch (ExecutionException e) {
        Throwable cause = e.getCause();
        System.out.println(cause.getClass().getName() + ": " + cause.getMessage());
        if (cause.getMessage() != null && cause.getMessage().contains("Unexpected status code: 307")) {
          System.exit(2);
        }
        throw e;
      } finally {
        transport.close();
      }
    } finally {
      server.stop(0);
    }
  }
}

    75	        httpVersion = builder.forceHttpVersion1_1 ? HttpClient.Version.HTTP_1_1 : HttpClient.Version.HTTP_2;
    76	        subsidiaryChannelEnabled = builder.subsidiaryChannelEnabled;
    77	        executor = getOrDefault(builder.executor, DefaultExecutorProvider.getDefaultExecutorService());
    78	        if (builder.httpClient != null) {
    79	            httpClient = builder.httpClient;
    80	            closeHttpClient = false;
    81	        } else {
    82	            HttpClient.Builder clientBuilder =
    83	                    HttpClient.newBuilder().connectTimeout(timeout).version(httpVersion);
    84	            if (builder.executor != null) {
    85	                clientBuilder.executor(builder.executor);
    86	            }
    87	            if (sslContext != null) {
    88	                clientBuilder.sslContext(sslContext);
    89	            }
    90	            if (builder.followRedirects != null) {
    91	                clientBuilder.followRedirects(builder.followRedirects);
    92	            }
    93	            httpClient = clientBuilder.build();
    94	            closeHttpClient = true;
    95	        }
    96	    }
   360	                    }
   361	                },
   362	                delayedExecutor);
   363	    }
   364	
   365	    private boolean isExpectedStatusCode(int statusCode) {
   366	        return statusCode >= 200 && statusCode < 300;
   367	    }
   368	
   369	    @Override
   370	    public void close() throws IOException {
   371	        closed.set(true);
   372	        if (!closeHttpClient) {
   373	            return;
   374	        }
   375	        // The httpClient.close() method only exists on JDK 21+, so invoke it only if we can.
   376	        // Replace this with a normal method call when switching the base to JDK 21+.
   377	        try {
   378	            httpClient.getClass().getMethod("close").invoke(httpClient);
   487	         */
   488	        public StreamableHttpMcpTransport.Builder sslContext(SSLContext sslContext) {
   489	            this.sslContext = sslContext;
   490	            return this;
   491	        }
